\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
API headers and documentation for the mmg3d library, for volumetric meshes in 3D. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Algiane Froehly (Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License.
\end{DoxyCopyright}
These are the API functions for the mmg3d library. These functions allow to load and save meshes and data defined on meshes; add, extract, or modify mesh data; and to call the library functions that perform remeshing, level-\/set discretization, and Lagrangian motion.

Meshes are here defined in terms of vertices and three-\/dimensional objects\+: tetrahedra and prisms. Optionally lower-\/dimensional entities can be present\+: triangles, quadrilaterals and edges. All of these {\itshape entities} can have a {\itshape reference\+:} an integer value that can serve as a group identifier. In addition mesh entities can have {\itshape attributes} such as \char`\"{}ridge\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}required\char`\"{}.

Data defined on meshes can be for example functions that are meant for level-\/set discretization, metric tensors that will govern edge lengths, and vector fields governing lagrangian motion. These data can be scalar, vector, or (symmetric) tensor-\/valued; and there can be more than one data item associated with a mesh entity. These data are often referred to as {\itshape solutions}.

Three of the functions here are referred to as \char`\"{}programs\char`\"{}, because they perform the tasks for which Mmg is meant\+: remeshing, level-\/set discretization and Lagrangian motion. The other functions merely serve to load and save data and to perform pre-\/ and post-\/processing. These programs actually behave much like independent programs\+: they send diagnostic output to stdout and in rare cases they may call the exit() function.



A very simple example code for mesh adaptation with automatic parsing of .mesh files

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_LMAX}{MMG3D\_LMAX}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+LMAX~10240}

Maximum array size when storing adjacent vertices (or ball) of a vertex.

\index{MMG3D\_Param@{MMG3D\_Param}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Param}{MMG3D\_Param}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg3d_8h_a964a06109019542d04f12263c3fae24d}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Param}}}



Input parameters for the mmg library. 

These are the input parameters for the mmg3d library functions. Options prefixed by {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+IPARAM} require integer values and options prefixed by {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+DPARAM} require real values. They can be set with the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_ad9d6a22f8d15fed615f67778f2a4f072}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+iparameter}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a4eb718dd5d69de7d8885d2a5d93f7bd2}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+dparameter}} functions, respectively. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron()}{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Add\+\_\+tetrahedron (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Add a tetrahedron to the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & first vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & second vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & third vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & fourth vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & tetrahedron reference.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function adds a tetrahedron with vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, {\itshape v3} and reference {\itshape ref} at the first available position of the mesh.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if unable to create the tetrahedron, the unit-\/offset index of the new tet if it has strictly positive volume, a negative index if it has a zero or negative volume.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv}}
\index{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv()}{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Compute\+\_\+eigenv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{m\mbox{[}6\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{lambda\mbox{[}3\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{vp\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symmetric matrix. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & upper part of a symmetric matrix diagonalizable in $\vert$R \\
\hline
{\em lambda} & array of the metric eigenvalues \\
\hline
{\em vp} & array of the metric eigenvectors\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the order of the eigenvalues
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symmetric matrix m whose upper part is provided (m11, m12, m13, m22, m23, m33 in this order).

lambda\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(1,\+:) in fortran

lambda\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(2,\+:) in fortran

lambda\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(3,\+:) in fortran

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+COMPUTE\+\_\+\+EIGENV(m,lambda,vp,retval)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: m($\ast$)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: lambda($\ast$),vp($\ast$)~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+adja\+Tet (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{kel,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{listet\mbox{[}4\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return adjacent elements of a tetrahedron. 

Utils 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em kel} & tetrahedron index. \\
\hline
{\em listet} & pointer to the array of the 4 tetra adjacent to {\itshape kel}. (the index is 0 if there is no adjacent) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Find the indices of the 4 adjacent elements of tetrahedron {\itshape kel}. $listet[i] = 0$ if the $i^{th}$ face has no adjacent element (so we are on a boundary face).

\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg3d_8h_afb23e92e9aa300f57ac40aef340f1c1b}\label{libmmg3d_8h_afb23e92e9aa300f57ac40aef340f1c1b}} 
\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_Get\_edge@{MMG3D\_Get\_edge}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_edge@{MMG3D\_Get\_edge}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_edge()}{MMG3D\_Get\_edge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Ridge,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next edge in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer to the first extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer to the second extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Ridge} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is ridge. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the extremities {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1} and reference {\itshape ref} of next edge of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all edges. When it has been called as many times as there are edges in the mesh, the internal edge counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

Get the vertices and references of all edges in a mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em edges} & pointer to the array of edges. The vertices of the $i^{th}$ edge are stored in edges\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$2\mbox{]} and edges\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$2+1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & edges references. refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]} is the ref of the $i^{th}$ edge. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Ridges} & 1 if the edge is a ridge, 0 otherwise. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Required} & 1 if the edge is required, 0 otherwise. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+ith\+Sol\+\_\+in\+Sols\+At\+Vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{i,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get one out of several solutions at a specific vertex. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to get. \\
\hline
{\em s} & solution(s) at mesh vertex {\itshape pos}. The required size of this array depends on the type of solution. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & index of the vertex on which we get the solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get values of the ith field of the solution array at vertex {\itshape pos}. (pos from 1 to nb\+\_\+vertices included and {\itshape i} from 1 to {\itshape nb\+\_\+sols}). The type of solution is inferred from {\itshape sol}.

 END SUBROUTINE~\newline

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_nonBdyTriangle()}{MMG3D\_Get\_nonBdyTriangle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+non\+Bdy\+Triangle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get vertices and reference of a non-\/boundary triangle. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the firts vertex of the triangle \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of the triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of the triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the triangle reference. \\
\hline
{\em idx} & index of the non-\/boundary triangle to get (between 1 and nb\+\_\+tria) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get vertices and reference {\itshape ref} of the idx$^\wedge$th non-\/boundary triangle (for DG methods for example). A tria is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references or if it belongs to one tetra only.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

Get the number of non-\/boundary triangles. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em nb\+\_\+tria} & pointer to the number of non-\/boundary triangles. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get the number of non-\/boundary triangles (for DG methods for example). A triangle is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references or if it belongs to one tetra only. Append these triangles to the list of triangles.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
reallocates the triangle array and appends the internal triangles. This may modify the behaviour of other functions.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+NUMBEROFNONBDYTRIANGLESS(mesh,nb\+\_\+tria,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: nb\+\_\+tria~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}
First step\+: Mesh analysis to detect the tetra/prisms boundary faces and to store the info in the xtetra/xprisms structures

Second step\+: Count the number of non boundary faces

Third step\+: Append the non boundary edges to the boundary edges array

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_prism()}{MMG3D\_Get\_prism()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+prism (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v4,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v5,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next prism in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & pointer to the fourth vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v4} & pointer to the fifth vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v5} & pointer to the sixth vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the prism reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if prism is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, {\itshape v3}, {\itshape v4}, {\itshape v5} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next prism of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all prisms. When it has been called as many times as there are prisms, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+PRISM(mesh,v0,v1,v2,v3,v4,v5,ref,is\+Required,\&~\newline
 retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: v0,v1,v2,v3,v4,v5~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\

{\em refs} & pointer to the array of the prism references. The reference of the $i^{th}$ prism is stored in refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}. \\

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol@{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tensor\+Sol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m11,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m12,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m13,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m22,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m23,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m33 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the next element of a tensor solution structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em m11} & pointer to the position (1,1) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m12} & pointer to the position (1,2) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m13} & pointer to the position (1,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m22} & pointer to the position (2,2) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m23} & pointer to the position (2,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m33} & pointer to the position (3,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the next element $(m_{11},m_{12},m_{13},m_{22},m_{23},m_{33})$ of a tensor-\/valued solution field. It is meant to be called in a loop over all vertices. When it has been called as many times as there are elements in the solution, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TENSORSOL(met,m11,m12,m13,m22,m23,m33,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: met~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: m11,m12,m13,m22,m23,m33~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

Get a tetrahedron given one of its triangles and the index by which it refers to this triangle (DEPRECATED). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em ktri} & index of the boundary triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ktet} & pointer to an integer that will contains the tetra index. \\
\hline

\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}
Fill {\itshape ktet} by the index of a tetrahedron to which belongs a boundary triangle and {\itshape iface} by the index of the triangle in the tetra.

will be deprecated in release 5.\+5

Get the vertices and reference of all tetrahedra in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em tetra} & pointer to the array where the vertices are to be stored. Vertices of the $i^{th}$ tetra are stored in tetra\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$4\mbox{]} to tetra\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$4+3\mbox{]} \\
\hline
{\em refs} & pointer to the array of the tetrahedron references. References of the $i^{th}$ tetra is stored in refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Required} & pointer to the array of the flags saying if the tetrahedra are required. are\+Required\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}=1 if the $i^{th}$ tetrahedron is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedron()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedron()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tetrahedron (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next tetrahedron in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & pointer to the fourth vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the tetrahedron reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if tetrahedron is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, {\itshape v3} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next tetrahedron of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all tetrahedra. When it has been called as many times as there are tetrahedra, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TETRAHEDRON(mesh,v0,v1,v2,v3,ref,is\+Required,\&~\newline
 retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: v0,v1,v2,v3~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} double MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tetrahedron\+Quality (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{k }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the quality measure of a single tetrahedron in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure (may be NULL for an isotropic metric). \\
\hline
{\em k} & index of the tetrahedron for which we want to get the quality (from 1 to the number of tetrahedra included) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the computed quality or 0 in case of failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function returns the quality measure of tetrahedron {\itshape k}. Quality values range from 0 (degenerate) to 1 (best attainable). The function returns 0 if the tetrahedron is flat or has a negative volume, and also if {\itshape k} is out of range. In the latter case it will also print a diagnostic message to standard output.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TETRAHEDRONQUALITY(mesh,met,k,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh,met~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: k~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tets\+From\+Tria (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ktri,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ktet\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},  }\item[{int}]{iface\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get two tetrahedra given a triangle and face indices. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em ktri} & index of the boundary triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ktet} & array of size 2 that will contain the indices of the tetra (filled by the function). \\
\hline
{\em iface} & pointer to an array of size 2 that will contains the indices of the faces of the tetras {\itshape ktet}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} that corresponds to the boundary tria {\itshape ktri}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Fill {\itshape ktet} by the indices of the tetrahedra that have a boundary triangle and {\itshape iface} by the indices of the faces of the tetras that correspond to the triangle. Fill ktet\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} and iface\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} by 0 if the triangle belongs to 1 tetrahedron only.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TETSFROMTRIA(mesh,ktri,ktet,iface,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: ktri~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), DIMENSION(2), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: ktet~\newline
 INTEGER, DIMENSION(2), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: iface~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+triangle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next triangle in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the triangle reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if triangle is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, and reference {\itshape ref} of the next triangle of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all triangles. When it has been called as many times as there are triangles, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vertex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c0,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c1,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Corner,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1},{\itshape c2} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next vertex of {\itshape mesh}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em c0} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the first dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c1} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the second dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c2} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the third dimension. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the vertex reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Corner} & pointer to the flag saying if vertex is corner. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if vertex is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1},{\itshape c2} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next vertex of a mesh. It is meant to be used in a loop over all vertices. When this function has been called as many times as there are vertices, the internal loop counter will be reset. To obtain data for a specific vertex, the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a04f98ce8620e83b2606115bfdf531b6c}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+By\+Idx\+\_\+vertex}} function can be used instead.

 INTEGER \+:: is\+Corner,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline

\end{quote}

Create array of adjacency. Set pack variable to 0 for a compact mesh and to 1 for a mesh that need to be packed.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Init\_mesh()}{MMG3D\_Init\_mesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int}]{starter,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize a mesh structure and optionally the associated solution and metric structures. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em starter} & dummy argument used to initialize the variadic argument list \\
\hline
{\em ...} & variadic arguments that depend on the library function that you want to call.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dlib function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a00ec28ed5d8e31f7c12cc1749403085c}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dls function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a00ec28ed5d8e31f7c12cc1749403085c}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dmov function, you must call \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met,\&empty\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp, \&your\+\_\+displacement, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here, {\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} and {\itshape your\+\_\+displacement} are \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 on success, 0 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function allocates and initializes MMG structures. All structures of types MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh and MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol that will be given as arguments to Mmg functions must be initialized with this function.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No fortran interface to allow variadic arguments.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
detected bugs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item some vertices along open boundaries end up with a normal (while they should not) 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyWarning}

Load a mesh and possibly a solution in .msh format from file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline

This function reads a mesh and 0 or 1 data fields in MSH file format (.msh extension). We read only low-\/order vertices, edges, triangles, quadrangles, tetrahedra and prisms.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+load\+Vtk\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a mesh and possibly a solution from a file in VTK format. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure or the NULL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the level-\/set structure or the NULL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if file is not found, -\/1 if fail for another reason (insufficient memory, file format...), 1 if success.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function reads a mesh and 0 or 1 data fields in VTK file format (.vtu extension). We read only low-\/order vertices, edges, tria, quadra, tetra and prisms. Point and cell references must be stored in Point\+Data or Cell\+Data whose names contain the \char`\"{}medit\+:ref\char`\"{} keyword.

\end{DoxyReturn}
Write mesh and 0 or 1 data in MSH file format (.msh extension). Write binary file for .mshb extension and ASCII for .msh one.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+save\+Msh\+Mesh\+\_\+and\+\_\+all\+Data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}} $\ast$}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Save a mesh and data in MSH format, ascii or binary depending on the filename extension. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the solution structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of file. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Write mesh and a list of data fields (that are considered as solutions and not metrics, thus, we do nothing over the ridge vertices) in MSH file format (.msh extension). Save file in ASCII format for .msh extension, in binary format for .mshb one.

\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_searchlen@{MMG3D\_searchlen}}
\index{MMG3D\_searchlen@{MMG3D\_searchlen}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_searchlen()}{MMG3D\_searchlen()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+searchlen (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double}]{lmin,  }\item[{double}]{lmax,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{eltab,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{met\+Rid\+Typ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



List edges that are too short or too long. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em lmin} & minimum edge length. \\
\hline
{\em lmax} & maximum ede length. \\
\hline
{\em eltab} & array of invalid elements. \\
\hline
{\em met\+Rid\+Typ} & Type of storage of ridges metrics\+: 0 for classic storage (before the MMG5\+\_\+defsiz call), 1 for special storage (after this call).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Store in {\itshape eltab} elements which have edge lengths shorter than {\itshape lmin} or longer than {\itshape lmax}, {\itshape eltab} is allocated and could contain {\itshape mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ne} elements.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: lmin,lmax~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT),DIMENSION($\ast$), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: eltab~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: metridtyp~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}{MMG3D\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ls\+Base\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{br }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a new level-\/set base reference. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em br} & new level-\/set base reference. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set a new level-\/set base reference of ref {\itshape br} in LS discretization mode. Base references are boundary conditions to which implicit domains can be attached. All implicit volumes that are not attached to listed base references are deleted as spurious volumes by the {\itshape rmc} option.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+LSBASEREFERENCE(mesh,sol,br,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: br~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+mesh\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{np,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ne,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{nprism,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{nt,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{nquad,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{na }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the number of vertices, tetrahedra, prisms, triangles, quadrilaterals, and edges of a mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em np} & number of vertices. \\
\hline
{\em ne} & number of tetrahedra. \\
\hline
{\em nprism} & number of prisms. \\
\hline
{\em nt} & number of triangles. \\
\hline
{\em nquad} & number of quads. \\
\hline
{\em na} & number of edges. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function sets the number of vertices, tetrahedra, prisms, triangles, quadrilaterals and edges of the mesh and allocates the associated arrays. If called again, it will reset the whole mesh to reallocate it at the new size

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+multi\+Mat (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref,  }\item[{int}]{split,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rplus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the reference mapping for the elements of reference {\itshape ref} in level-\/set discretization mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure \\
\hline
{\em ref} & input tetrahedron reference \\
\hline
{\em split} & MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+No\+Split if the entity must not be splitted, MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+Split otherwise \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & reference for the negative side after LS discretization \\
\hline
{\em rplus} & reference for the positive side after LS discretization \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+MULTIMAT(mesh,sol,ref,split,rmin,rplus,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh,sol~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: split~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: ref,rmin,rplus~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}
With this function you can determine which references will be given to the tetrahedra on both sides of the level set, after discretization. Negative and positive here refer to volumes where the function is smaller or larger, respectively, than the isovalue of the level set. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

Initialize a solution field. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em typ\+Entity} & type of entities on which the solution is defined (vertices, triangles, ...). See \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_ad7dceff255dbd127a2b7ff2ceb8d9ba6}{MMG5\+\_\+entities}} for the defined entity types. Currently only \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_ad7dceff255dbd127a2b7ff2ceb8d9ba6a3e0b7e1298beaabada671bf465c477c2}{MMG5\+\_\+\+Vertex}} is supported. \\
\hline
{\em np} & number of solutions. \\
\hline
{\em typ\+Sol} & type of solution (scalar, vectorial, ..., see \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a68ad1024791ce7577a19c0ee1dde271e}{MMG5\+\_\+type}} for possible values). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Initialize a solution field\+: set dimension, types and number of data. To use to initialize a metric, a level-\/set or a displacement field.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+tetrahedra (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{tetra,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the vertices and references of all tetrahedra in a mesh structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em tetra} & vertices of the tetras of the mesh given. The vertices of the $i^{th}$ tetrahedron are given by tetra\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$4\mbox{]} to tetra\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$4+3\mbox{]} included. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & array of the tetrahedra references. The references of the $i^{th}$ tetrahedron is given by refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function sets the vertices and references of all tetrahedra in a mesh.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+tetrahedron (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



set a single tetrahedron\textquotesingle{}s vertices 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & first vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & second vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & third vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & fourth vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & tetrahedron reference. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & tetrahedron position in the mesh. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Assign the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1},{\itshape v2},{\itshape v3} and reference {\itshape ref} to the tetrahedron at position {\itshape pos} in the mesh structure. {\itshape pos} ranges from 1 to nb\+\_\+tetra included.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} double($\ast$ MMG3\+D\+\_\+lenedg\+Coor) (double $\ast$ca, double $\ast$cb, double $\ast$sa, double $\ast$sb) (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double $\ast$}]{ca,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{cb,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{sa,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{sb }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Compute the length of an edge according to the size prescription. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ca} & pointer to the coordinates of the first edge\textquotesingle{}s extremity. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & pointer to the coordinates of the second edge\textquotesingle{}s extremity. \\
\hline
{\em ma} & pointer to the metric associated to the first edge\textquotesingle{}s extremity. \\
\hline
{\em mb} & pointer to the metric associated to the second edge\textquotesingle{}s extremity. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
edge length.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the length of edge $[ca,cb]$ (with {\itshape ca} and {\itshape cb} coordinates of edge endpoints) according to the size prescription.
